Print out an HTML "{}$<$select$>$"{} for a dropdown

This should be overloaded in Class


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
array & {\em \$options} & array of possible options\+: Parameters which could be used in options array \+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item name \+: string / name of the select (default is depending itemtype)
\item value \+: integer / preselected value (default 0)
\item comments \+: boolean / is the comments displayed near the dropdown (default true)
\item entity \+: integer or array / restrict to a defined entity or array of entities (default -\/1 \+: no restriction)
\item toupdate \+: array / \doxylink{class_update}{Update} a specific item on select change on dropdown (need value\+\_\+fieldname, to\+\_\+update, url (see Ajax\+::update\+Item\+On\+Select\+Event for information) and may have moreparams)
\item used \+: array / Already used items ID\+: not to display in dropdown (default empty)
\item hide\+\_\+if\+\_\+no\+\_\+elements \+: boolean / hide dropdown if there is no elements (default false)
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\item noid Set to true if ID should not be append (eg. already done in formtitle)
